### [Vector Floating-Point Absolute Value Functions](../rvv-intrinsic-api.md#1412-vector-floating-point-sign-injection-operations):

**Prototypes:**

### [Narrowing Floating-Point/Integer Type-Convert Functions](../rvv-intrinsic-api.md#1419-narrowing-floating-pointinteger-type-convert-operations):

**Prototypes:**
